    name AS name,
    rank AS rank
FROM
    jp_company
WHERE
     cate=2 
ORDER BY
    rank DESC
LIMIT 10

2022-09-13T23:45:36 select u.username,c.j_company as name,SUM(a.count_shu) as ying_shu,a.k_id,tt.yi_shu,(SUM(a.count_shu)-tt.yi_shu) as ying_fu from jp_bill as a
left join 
(
select SUM(money) as yi_shu,comid from jp_finc 
where cate=0   
group by comid
) as tt on a.k_id=tt.comid
left join jp_customer as c on c.id=a.k_id
left join jp_sysmember as u on u.id=a.b_busid

where    1=1  and a.b_busid=1 group by a.k_id order by convert(u.username USING gbk) COLLATE gbk_chinese_ci

2022-09-13T23:45:38 SELECT
    COUNT(a.id) AS genvid
FROM
    jp_bill a
LEFT JOIN jp_customer b ON a.k_id=b.id
WHERE
     status in( 0,1,2,3,4,5 ) and (b_busid in(1,88,82,115,75,76,68,120,111,113,110,118) or b_opeid in(1,88,82,115,75,76,68,120,111,113,110,118) )
LIMIT 1  
2022-09-13T23:45:39 SELECT
    a.id AS id,
    a.k_id AS k_id,
    a.b_code AS b_code,
    a.pc_port AS pc_port,
    a.count_shu AS count_shu,
    a.count_zhi AS count_zhi,
    a.account AS account,
    a.postdate AS postdate,
    a.finshdate AS finshdate,
    a.editdate AS editdate,
    a.status AS status,
    a.b_opeid AS b_opeid,
    a.b_busid AS b_busid,
    a.b_product_name AS b_product_name,
    a.b_tank_code AS b_tank_code,
    a.shi_shu AS shi_shu,
    a.shi_zhi AS shi_zhi,
    b.j_company AS j_company
FROM
    jp_bill a
LEFT JOIN jp_customer b ON a.k_id=b.id
WHERE
     status in( 0,1,2,3,4,5 ) and (b_busid in(1,88,82,115,75,76,68,120,111,113,110,118) or b_opeid in(1,88,82,115,75,76,68,120,111,113,110,118) )
ORDER BY
    a.id DESC
LIMIT 10

2022-09-13T23:45:39 SELECT
    a.roleid AS roleid,
    a.groupid AS groupid,
    a.menuid AS menuid,
    a.actid AS actid,
    c.appname AS app,
    c.name AS act
FROM
    jp_syspower a
LEFT JOIN jp_sysnode c ON a.actid=c.md5key
WHERE
    roleid in(1) and actid!='0'
